event = {
	id = 2003005
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = FRA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = FRA }
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = {
			garrison = { country = GER province = 126 size = 1 } #aachen
			garrison = { country = GER province = 131 size = 1 } #kln
			garrison = { country = GER province = 129 size = 1 } #koblenz
			garrison = { country = GER province = 128 size = 1 } #Trier
			garrison = { country = GER province = 127 size = 1 } #Saarbrücken
			garrison = { country = GER province = 130 size = 1 } #Mainz
			garrison = { country = GER province = 136 size = 1 } #Karlsruhe
			garrison = { country = GER province = 132 size = 1 } #Freiburg
			garrison = { country = GER province = 145 size = 1 } #Essen
			garrison = { country = GER province = 139 size = 1 } #Darmstadt
			garrison = { country = GER province = 142 size = 1 } #Duesseldorf
			garrison = { country = GER province = 143 size = 1 } #Neuwied
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = FRA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = FRA }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { ai = yes random = 3 }		
			AND = { 
				ai = no
				OR = {
					garrison = { country = GER province = 126 size = 1 } #aachen
					garrison = { country = GER province = 131 size = 1 } #kln
					garrison = { country = GER province = 129 size = 1 } #koblenz
					garrison = { country = GER province = 128 size = 1 } #Trier
					garrison = { country = GER province = 127 size = 1 } #Saarbrücken
					garrison = { country = GER province = 130 size = 1 } #Mainz
					garrison = { country = GER province = 136 size = 1 } #Karlsruhe
					garrison = { country = GER province = 132 size = 1 } #Freiburg
					garrison = { country = GER province = 145 size = 1 } #Essen
					garrison = { country = GER province = 139 size = 1 } #Darmstadt
				}
			}
		}
	}
   
	name = "EVT_2000_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_2000_DESC" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Rhineland"
	decision_picture = "decision_Rhineland"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "2003005a"
		command = { type = relation which = FRA value = -15 }
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = BEL value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = HOL value = -5 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = money value = 500 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = 10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2001025 } # UK Gears up for war
		command = { type = trigger which = 2002001 } # France Gears up for war
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = FRA country = BEL } } type = trigger which = 2015008 } # Belgium leaves the Allies
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = ai which = "switch/GER_Rhine.ai" }
	}
}

#########################################################################
#  Anti-Comintern Pact
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 2003007
	random = no
	country = GER

	name = EVT_71_NAME
	desc = EVT_71_DESC
  	style = 2
  	picture = "Pact_of_Steel"
	decision_picture = "decision_anticominternpact"

	decision = {
		exists = JAP
		exists = ITA
		exists = SOV
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { war = { country = ITA country = ETH } }
			war = { country = SPA country = SPR } 
			year = 1937
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { war = { country = ITA country = ETH } }
			AND = { war = { country = SPA country = SPR } random = 50 } 
			year = 1937
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = EVT_71_ACTA
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -50 }
		command = { type = setflag which = anti_comintern_pact }
 		command = { type = removecore which = 401 } # Trento
 		command = { type = removecore which = 402 } # Bolzano
		
	}
}

	id = 2006001
	random = no
	country = ITA

	decision = {
		event = 2003007
		exists = GER
		exists = SOV
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = {
			alliance = { country = GER country = ITA }
			year = 1938
			event = 2011021 #JAP  Seek German recognition of Manchukuo
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			alliance = { country = GER country = ITA }
			AND = {
				flag = JAP_Anti_comintern_pact
				random = 10
			}
			AND = {	
				flag = NO_JAP_Anti_comintern_pact
				random = 5
			}
			AND = {
				#much more likely to fire after historical date
				month = 3
				year = 1938
				random = 90
			}
		}
		exists = GER
		exists = SOV
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	name = EVT_72_NAME
	desc = 72desc
	style = 2
  	picture = "Pact_of_Steel"
	
	decision_picture = "decision_anticominternpact"

		command = { type = end_guarantee which = ITA where = AUS }
		command = { type = setflag which = ITA_Anti_comintern_pact }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2003008 }
	}
}

			control = { province = 197 data = CZE }

			control = { province = 200 data = CZE }
			control = { province = 206 data = CZE }
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				war = { country = CZE country = GER }
				alliance = { country = CZE country = GER }
				ispuppet = GER
				puppet = { country = CZE country = GER }
			}
		}
	}

		}

			OR = {
				exists = SLO			
				ispuppet = CZE
				alliance = { country = CZE country = GER }
				alliance = { country = CZE country = SOV }

		}
	}

		command = { type = trigger which = 2003016 } # GER
	}

event = {
	id = 2003021
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = {
		atwar = no
		control = { province = 261 data = LIT } # Klaipedia			
		OR = { 
			event = 2003015 
			event = 2003013 
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { month = june year = 1939 } 		
			event = { id = 2003015 days = 15 } 
			event = { id = 2003013 days = 180 } 
		}
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = LIT } }
		NOT = { ispuppet = LIT }
		NOT = { ispuppet = GER }
		#NOT = { event = 2007018 } # Mol-Rib pact
		garrison = { country = GER province = 184 size = 1 } # Königsberg
	}
	
	trigger = {
		atwar = no
		NOT = { event = 2007018 } # Mol-Rib pact
		control = { province = 261 data = LIT } # Klaipedia
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				ispuppet = LIT
				ispuppet = GER			
				alliance = { country = GER country = LIT }
			}
		}		
		OR = { 
			random = 6 
			AND = { 
				month = june 
				year = 1939 
				random = 50 
			} 
		}
		OR = { 
			event = 2003015 
			event = 2003013 
		}		
	}

	name = "EVT_2008_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_2008_DESC"
  	style = 2
  	picture = "Memel"
	decision_picture = "decision_Memel"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 12
	deathdate = { day = 12 month = march year = 1966 }

	action = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME2008A"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = addcore which = 261 } # Klaipeda - Baltic States
		command = { type = trigger which = 2029001 } # LIT
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = LIT value = -40 }
	}

event = {
	id = 2003024
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = {
		exists = POL	
		exists = SOV
		OR = { 
			AND = { month = september year = 1939 } 		
			event = { id = 2003015 days = 144 } 
			event = { id = 2003013 days = 300 } 
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				ispuppet = POL			
				ispuppet = GER
				ispuppet = SOV		
				war = { country = SOV country = GER }
				alliance = { country = GER country = POL }
				alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			}
		}		
	}
	decision_trigger = { 
		#OR = { 
		#	AND = { difficulty = 3 relation = { which = SOV value = 50 } }
		#	AND = { NOT = { difficulty = 3 } relation = { which = SOV value = -50 } }
		#}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		exists = POL	
		exists = SOV
		OR = {

			}

		}

			alliance = { country = GER country = AUS }
		}

			event = 2003011 # Germany demands Sudetenland
			event = 2003107 #fall grün

		}

			OR = {
				alliance = { country = GER country = POL }
				war = { country = GER country = POL }
				puppet = { country = POL country = GER }
				ispuppet = GER
			}
		}
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 181 data = GER } } # Danzig
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = POL } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = POL } }
		NOT = { puppet = { country = POL country = GER } }
		NOT = { ispuppet = GER }
	}
	
	trigger = {
		#random = 50 #Having this be random delays this too much
		government = fascist

# Fall Weserübung
event = {
	id = 2003067
	random = no
	country = GER

	name = 29name
	desc = 29desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Fall_Weserubung"

	decision = {
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }		
		OR = {
			owned = { province = 232 data = -3 } #Warsaw owned by friendly nation
			event = { id = 2003036 days = 30 }
		}
		OR = {
			exists = NOR
			exists = DEN	
		}
		NOT = {
			atwar = NOR
			atwar = DEN
			alliance = { country = GER country = DEN } 
			alliance = { country = GER country = NOR }  			
		}                                
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = { 
		event = { id = 2003036 days = 120 }
		alliance = { country = GER country = POL }
		}
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = DEN } }  
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = NOR } }               
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = { 
			AND = {
				random = 10 
				transport_plane = { country = -1 value = 1 }
				transport = { country = GER value = 3 }
				}
			AND = {
				random = 40 
				transport_plane = { country = -1 value = 3 }
				transport = { country = GER value = 5 }
				}
			AND = { 
				year = 1940 
				month = 3
				random = 50 
			}
			AND = {
				naval_percentage = { country = ENG value = 0.8 }
				land_percentage = { country = FRA value = 1.1 }
				transport = { country = GER value = 4 } 
				}
		}
		OR = {
			event = { id = 2003036 days = 90 }
			alliance = { country = GER country = POL }
		}
		OR = {
			exists = NOR
			exists = DEN	
		}
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }		
		NOT = {
			atwar = NOR
			atwar = DEN
			alliance = { country = SOV country = DEN }
			alliance = { country = SOV country = NOR }
			alliance = { country = GER country = DEN }
			alliance = { country = GER country = NOR }
		}                  
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }                  
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 6
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = january year = 1960 }

	action_a = {
		name = 29a
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = war which = NOR }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = war which = DEN }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = ai_prepare_war which = NOR }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = ai_prepare_war which = DEN }
		command = { type = relation which = DEN value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = NOR value = -10 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = ENG NOT = { flag = AlliesSouth } } type = trigger which = 3001074 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2003116
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		exists = HUN
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		OR = { 
			war = { country = GER country = YUG }
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			war = { country = GER country = GRE }			
		}
		NOT = { alliance = { country = HUN country = GER } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = HUN country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = GER } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = ITA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = SOV } }
	}

	decision_trigger = {
	 	relation = { which = HUN value = 50 }
		event = 2003047 # German diplomatic offensive
		OR = {
			garrison = { country = -1 province = 188 type = land size = 9 area = 1 }  # Eisenstadt, Austria Area
			garrison = { country = -1 province = 208 type = land size = 9 area = 1 }  # Bratislava, Slovakia Area
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		random = 10
		exists = HUN
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		OR = { 
			war = { country = GER country = YUG }
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			war = { country = GER country = GRE }			
		}
		NOT = { alliance = { country = HUN country = GER } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = HUN country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = GER } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = ITA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = HUN country = SOV } }
	}

	desc = 2003112desc
  	style = 2
  	picture = "hungary_axis"

	}

		command = { }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2003178
	random = no
	country = GER

	name = EVT_2003178_NAME
	desc = EVT_2003178_DESC
	style = 2
  	picture = "wunderwaffen"
  	decision_picture = "decision_wunderwaffen"

	decision = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
			OR = { war = { country = GER country = USA } war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = { 
		money = 5000 
		#incabinet = 88 # Goebbels as Minister of Security
		OR = { region = { region = Norway country = -3 } rocket_test = 2 }
	}	
	
	trigger = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
			OR = { war = { country = GER country = USA } war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
			OR = {
				year = 1943
				random = 30 # Give a small chance to trigger this in 1942
			}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1942 }
	offset = 80
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		trigger = { OR = { ai = yes rocket_test = 2 } }
		ai_chance = 50
		name = EVT_2003178_ACTIONA # Flying Bombs and Rockets
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 5560 } # Experimental Rocket Engine
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7550 } # Rocket Test and Research Facility
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7560 } # Practical Rocket Engine
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7570 } # Experimental Turbojet Engine
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7580 } # Flying Bomb Development
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7590 } # Flying Rocket Development
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7100 } # Flying Bomb
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 7110 } # Flying Rocket
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -5000 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = { OR = { ai = yes region = { region = Norway country = -3 } } }
		ai_chance = 50
		name = EVT_2003178_ACTIONB # A Nazi Nuclear Bomb
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 5500 } # Isotope Separation Facility
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 5510 } # Nuclear Fuel Analysis
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 5520 } # Experimental Reactor

		command = { type = gain_tech which = 5540 } # Nuclear Power Production

# Elser Bomb Plot
event = {
	id = 2003180
	random = no
	country = GER
	one_action = yes

	trigger = {
		government = fascist
		headofstate = 1
		atwar = yes
		control = { province = 179 data = GER } # Munich (the plot was possible only because of the annual speech at Munich's Burgerbraukeller)
		random = 95
		month = november
		NOT = { month = december }
			
	}

	name = 2003180name
	desc = 2003180desc
	style = 2
	picture = "elser_bomb_plot"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 93 
		name = 2003180a
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 } #Hitler actually was able to strengthen his power with all the propaganda and destiny mishmash after the attempt
	}
	action = {
		trigger = { ai = no OR = { difficulty = 3 difficulty = 4 } } #Fire only on strong / very strong allies
		ai_chance = 7
		name = 2003180b
		command = { type = headofstate which = 11 } # Hermann Göring (at that time, he had been appointed as the successor of Hitler)
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 21 } # Hermann Göring
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 1 } # Adolf Hitler
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = remove_division which = 14500 value = 1080 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 1000500 }
	}
}

#### Event ideas -
#### London gun - build it via decision, random chance to damage london afterwards
#### Mainstein's Plan - Tank bonus for forests and hills, lasts ~10 days when DOWing Netherlands and Belgium
#### Goering's Ambition - Land unit malus & slight dive bomber buff for ~10 days when entering France and reaching coast
